Germany Designates Demilitarized Zone along the Borders of Belgium, France, and Czechoslovakia; Soldiers in Uniform Not Permitted Within Five Kilometers; Rhineland is Exempt 60

Berlin Minister of Defense General von Blomberg recently issued an order designating a zone within five kilometers of the borders of France, Belgium, and Czechoslovakia where German army officers and soldiers are not permitted to enter in uniform. The Rhineland area is an exception. However, the above measures still apply to bridges over rivers connecting France and Germany. In cases where soldiers are given leave and travel to the aforementioned areas within five kilometers for vacation, the relevant commander may make special accommodations to allow them to enter. The aforementioned order was published in the government gazette on May 1st. Its nature is no different from establishing new demilitarized zones near the borders of the three countries. (Havas dispatch on the 5th)

Egypt's Young New King Returns to Cairo from England; The Late King's Sixty-Year-Old Nephew is Established as Crown Prince 61

Cairo The new King Farouk arrived in the capital today. The public was extremely excited. When the new King emerged from the station, the public cheered and a 21-gun salute was fired. The new King then traveled by car to the great mosque where he prayed at his father's mausoleum. (Reuters dispatch on the 6th)

Cairo Today, the cabinet ordered that Prince Muhammad Ali, the nephew of the late King Fuad, be the Crown Prince. The prince is currently sixty years old and studied in Geneva and Vienna. The prince enjoys traveling. He went to England at the age of six. The prince has visited the courts of various European countries. He first met Queen Victoria, when Gladstone was Prime Minister, and then went to Paris and other capitals. He also traveled to Russia, when Alexander III was Emperor. The Prince is an artist. He often paints in his garden and has held exhibitions in Cairo. He often gives paintings to British friends, so several homes in the English countryside have his works on display. (Reuters dispatch on the 6th)

Japanese Parliament Opens; Foreign Minister Arita Delivers Speech on Diplomatic Policy; Still the "Three Principles" towards China; Hamada Questions Diplomatic Results, Saying They Cannot Be Achieved by the Military 62

(Tokyo) The House of Representatives meeting began at 1:20 pm today. There was almost no space to stand in the gallery. Prime Minister Hirota, with a solemn attitude, ascended the podium, placed his hands on the table, and focused on his draft to deliver a policy speech. His words were the same as those in the House of Peers.

Next, Foreign Minister Arita delivered a speech. When he stated that the Soviet Union, in a distant location, is strengthening its massive military, we cannot help but be concerned, the entire audience clapped to express their enthusiastic support. Then, Minister of Finance Baba ascended the podium. He was quite nervous as he first came on stage. After reading the speech, then Minister of the Army Terauchi, amidst cheers, ascended the stage, and in the simple tone of a military man, reported on the progress of the February 26th Incident.

At 2:35 pm, Diet members began to question the speeches of the Ministers of State. First, Nakayama Matsuju (Minseito) briefly stated that the February 26th Incident was related to communist ideology. The government should dispel the public's doubts and finally called for freedom of speech, the abolition of martial law, and that the Japanese nation should seek development overseas. At this time, the Prime Minister returned to the stage to make a simple reply, causing a commotion in the Diet. Then the Home Minister, seeing that the situation was not good, went on stage to give a perfunctory response. At 3:20 pm, Hamada Kunimatsu (Seiyukai) made the second round of questioning, saying that the government should not focus too much on material politics but should focus on spiritual politics. He also spoke about diplomatic policy as follows:

Japan is the third most populous country in the world, but its resources are weak, so it must demand a redistribution of world resources for its own sake. Japanese national defense must enable diplomacy to achieve the above results and provide assistance. This cannot be achieved by a military that only engages in war.

Finally, regarding Minister of the Army Terauchi's statement, he questioned his so-called military's economic control and the mindset of the opinion letter on the uprising of the rebel army. He descended the stage at 4:30 pm. The Minister of the Army replied as follows:

The purpose of the statement is to correct capitalism and implement a totalitarian economy. As for the opinion letter on the February 26th Incident, it is entirely difficult to agree with.

The Minister of Education and the Prime Minister also answered in agreement. Speaker Tomita then declared a closed meeting to be held. It was already 5 pm. (Domei News Agency dispatch on the 6th)

Full Text of Arita's Speech 63

(Tokyo) Foreign Minister Arita delivered a speech on diplomatic policy at the House of Peers at 11 am on the 6th. The full text is as follows:

At this time of many domestic and foreign affairs, it is my honor to assume the heavy responsibility of foreign policy and to present my views on Japanese diplomatic policy here today. To ensure the stability of East Asia to contribute to world peace, and at the same time establish international justice and promote human welfare, is the national policy of Japan. I believe that ensuring the survival of the Japanese people, expecting their development, and at the same time attempting to harmonize all countries, especially with the inseparable relationship between Japan and Manchukuo as a foundation, to establish Japan as a stabilizing force in East Asia, is the guiding spirit of Japanese diplomacy to implement the above national policy.

When handling international cases under this national policy and guiding spirit, a self-reliant and active attitude should be adopted and damage to the character of a great power like Japan should be avoided. In order to comply with the Emperor's decree regarding withdrawal from the League of Nations, "Firmly believe in internationality and promote great righteousness in the universe." Observing the current international situation, the world is filled with an atmosphere of anxiety and dissatisfaction everywhere, and situations that will disrupt peace appear everywhere. Therefore, the first step is to eliminate the causes of such anxiety and dissatisfaction. This is the reason for ensuring world peace, and it goes without saying. It is natural for countries to focus on protecting their own interests, but because they are so loyal to this, they have not fully understood the positions of other countries. This is the cause of the world's anxiety and dissatisfaction. I firmly believe that politicians from various countries should think about this and adjust political and economic relations.

Starting with Boundary Demarcation in Relations with Russia 64

Regarding Japan's relations with other countries, I intend to gradually present my views below. For the sake of maintaining peace in East Asia, the Japanese government hopes that the relationship between Japan, Manchuria, and the Soviet Union will be normal and stable. It goes without saying that the Japanese government and the government of "Manchukuo" have no intention of aggression whatsoever. However, recently, incidents continue to occur on the border between "Manchukuo" and the Soviet Union, and similar incidents have also occurred between "Manchukuo" and Outer Mongolia, which is regrettable. In particular, the lack of a clear border line, based on one-sided judgments, recognizes the fact of border crossings, and immediately uses weapons, which does not provide any practical benefit other than sharpening diplomatic relations. The Japanese government has requested the Soviet government authorities to pay attention to such actions, and now takes this opportunity to urge the Soviet government to reflect more vigorously. As a result of consultations between the Japanese government and the "Manchukuo" government, in mid-March, it proposed to the Soviet government to take effective and appropriate measures to clarify the entire border line between Manchuria and the Soviet Union. At the same time, it proposed to establish a mechanism for the peaceful resolution of border disputes, and advocated that it should first start in the eastern border area where the most disputes occur, from Xingkai Lake to the Tumen River. In view of the fact that recent Manchurian-Soviet border incidents have almost occurred in this area, we believe that the Soviet government will quickly agree to this practical proposal from Japan, and that country's government has already expressed its intention to agree. We hope to gradually see the progress of concrete consultations.

Regarding the relationship between "Manchukuo" and Outer Mongolia, negotiations are currently being conducted directly between Manchuria and Mongolia. It is reported that "Manchukuo" is attempting to peacefully resolve various outstanding issues in accordance with the progress of these negotiations, in order to establish good neighborly and friendly relations. The Japanese government hopes that direct negotiations between Manchuria and Mongolia will quickly resolve various outstanding issues, and even lead to the exchange of representatives from both sides. As a result of the above explanation, you can infer the current state of Japanese-Soviet relations, which cannot be said to be clear. To put it bluntly, the root cause lies in the Soviet Union's lack of understanding of Japan's position in East Asia, and its suspicion of Japan. The Soviet Union's excessive military deployment in the Far Eastern border area poses a threat to peace in East Asia. We hereby declare clearly that the Japanese government, out of a sincere hope for peace in East Asia, cannot but have serious concerns about the above facts.

Regarding "Manchukuo," based on the inseparable relationship between Japan and that country, and in accordance with the diplomatic policy of establishing normal relations between Japan, China, and Manchuria, we are doing our utmost to assist in the economic development and other undertakings of "Manchukuo." At the same time, regarding the abolition of extraterritorial rights of Japan in various countries, and the adjustment, and even transfer, of administrative rights over the South Manchuria Railway affiliated land, preparations are currently underway to gradually realize this plan.

No Abandonment of Three Principles Towards China 65

As for Sino-Japanese relations, Foreign Minister Hirota has already explained in detail at the 68th Imperial Diet that negotiations will be conducted between China and Japan on the basis of the Three Principles towards China. In order to conduct negotiations on this basis, the Chinese authorities should understand the overall situation in East Asia, and make a major determination to undertake these negotiations. Unfortunately, it seems that the Chinese side does not have this full determination, which is regrettable. However, the adjustment of Sino-Japanese relations is not only extremely necessary for China and Japan, but also for peace in East Asia. Therefore, I demand a determination from the Chinese side, and at the same time, I intend to do my best to adjust Sino-Japanese relations in all aspects so that there are no regrets. The Japanese government has always paid close attention to the intrusion of red forces into East Asia. According to external reports, a part of the main force of the Communist army that previously moved from Sichuan Province to Shaanxi Province has recently invaded Shanxi Province and continues to operate, and depending on future developments, it seems to have a posture of advancing further north. The Japanese government pays great attention to this fact.

Maintaining Friendly Relations with England 66

When His Majesty King George V of England passed away on January 20, the late King reigned over the British Empire for 25 years. During this period, he dealt with the world war and other difficult and complex situations at home and abroad, and was a famous monarch praised for his wisdom and virtue. His Majesty the new King Edward VIII has long had a good understanding of the complex international political situation and has visited Japan. I hope that the future of the British Empire will be even more fortunate under the rule of the new King, and that the traditional friendly relations between Japan and England will be further enhanced. Japan and England have many common interests to investigate in various aspects of the world. However, based on the traditional friendship between Japan and England and the two countries' responsibility for world peace, and with full consideration of their respective special needs, the adjustment of their interests is by no means difficult.

Making Efforts to Promote Understanding with the United States 67

It goes without saying that the friendly relations between Japan and the United States are the key to peace in the Pacific. Japan and the United States not only have an interdependent economic relationship at present, but also the understanding between the two peoples is gradually deepening, which is what we are most pleased about. In the future, the two countries should respect each other's positions and missions, and work together to ensure peace in the Pacific. Regarding the understanding and friendship between the two countries, I intend to make further and better efforts.

Advocating Abolition of Economic Armaments 68

Secondly, observing the current state of international trade, in various foreign countries, various excuses are used to attempt to exclude foreign products, or so-called economic alliances are formed by several countries, and the trend of solidifying economic armaments is becoming more and more obvious. The Japanese government believes that if this trend is allowed to continue, the world's economic downturn will become more profound, and in the end, it will lead to the shrinking of world trade, resulting in the regression of human economic life. At every opportunity, it advocates to various countries to abolish this so-called economic armament, which can open up the world's economic downturn, and can contribute to the coexistence and co-prosperity of nations and world peace. However, Japan's advocacy has unfortunately not been accepted by most countries, and the establishment of obstacles to international trade has a tendency to expand its scope. In particular, among various foreign countries, there are those who specialize in suppressing Japanese goods, which is a major problem for countries like Japan that need to secure the supply of raw materials and the sales routes of products overseas in order to maintain the survival of the national economy. Japan should make efforts to abolish the above-mentioned economic armaments in a friendly manner, and when Japan's efforts cannot improve the situation, Japan will have no choice but to take necessary measures to deal with it. At this time, Japan's purpose is, of course, only to request the provinces of the other country to have satisfactory international trade relations, and there is no other intention.

Promoting Profound Oriental Culture 69

Finally, I would like to say a word about the issue of culture and international relations. In order to promote international understanding and friendship, the introduction of culture is extremely important, which goes without saying. In addition to the existing cultural undertakings with China, the Japanese government has established international cultural undertakings since the ninth year of Showa (1934) and has been working hard to expand them. As a result, foreign nationals studying Japan are becoming increasingly enthusiastic, and in the future, we should also strive to promote this kind of undertaking in order to deepen international understanding, promote world culture, and contribute to the enhancement of human welfare. In addition, we will improve various facilities for the existing cultural undertakings with China in order to promote cultural cooperation between China, Japan, and Manchuria, and promote the profound and profound oriental culture.

Tokyo Incident Affects Diplomacy 70

The unfortunate incident that occurred in the capital had a great impact on foreign countries and affected Japan's foreign relations. However, with the promulgation of the Emperor's dignity and the promotion of the spirit of national service, the situation was resolved and nothing happened, which can be said to be fortunate in misfortune. I firmly believe that the way to overcome the difficulties of the times and implement national policies lies in the full understanding of the international situation and the concerted efforts of all parties in the government and the public to advance towards their goals. I sincerely hope that you will provide enthusiastic assistance, and at the same time, I expect you to make the greatest efforts to fulfill your important responsibilities. (6th Allied Press Telegram)

Summary of Hirota's Speech 71

(Tokyo) Prime Minister Hirota gave a speech in the House of Peers today, the gist of which is as follows:

At the opening ceremony the other day, I received gracious words from the Emperor, which I was extremely frightened and grateful for. The unfortunate incident occurred on February 26, which is regrettable for all the people. However, this was only the action of a few elements in the military and outsiders. I believe that the foundation of the national army will never be shaken by this occurrence. However, if the national conscription obligation is doubted by this incident, and there is unrest among the people who support the military, then this is a major event for the country. We hope that the military will clarify the true meaning of the national army and rectify military discipline with a strong determination. The government also intends to work with the military to renovate national policies and maintain the dignity of the national constitution and laws when this goal is achieved, which is an extremely urgent task in the current situation.

Japan's constitutional politics is a legitimate political system stipulated by the constitution. The government should adopt a political program, as stated at the beginning of the cabinet formation. In Japan, glorifying the ideals of the founding of the nation and realizing the beauty of a unified nation with one monarch and all the people are the basis of domestic and foreign politics. Therefore, the clear demonstration of the concept of national polity is an urgent task at present.

Japan's consistent diplomatic policy is based on international trust, with the aim of contributing to world peace and human welfare by exerting its power to stabilize East Asia. With this aim, the government intends to establish an active and independent diplomacy. The Soviet Union makes inappropriate speculations about the Japanese Empire and implements excessive military preparations in the Far East, which is something that Japan finds difficult to understand. We sincerely hope that the Soviet Union will strive to ease this situation.

The Chinese political situation has recently maintained a relatively calm state, which the Japanese government is very pleased about. The government's policy towards China will be implemented without regret, so that China can correct its anti-Japanese and anti-Manchu attitude and promote friendship and cooperation between China, Japan, and Manchuria. We hope that the Chinese government will respond to the Japanese government's sincere expectations as soon as possible, and actively cooperate to achieve this common goal. In view of the current state of the international situation, the government will pay attention to the trends of various countries, and strive to enrich national defense and related equipment maintenance, in order to eliminate anxieties about national defense. At the same time, based on the broad concept of national defense, we will actively prepare for the cultivation, control, and utilization of Japanese resources. Observing the progress of national fortune and the current internal and external situation, there are many important national policies that need to be implemented, and reforms of the tax system and improvements in finance are particularly necessary for the renovation of financial economy.

At present, the finances of local organizations are extremely poor, making the local economy increasingly exhausted. The government will study fundamental ways to improve local finances, and regarding the harmony between national defense and industry, the construction of important industries, the revitalization of rural areas, the promotion of small and medium-sized commercial industries, and the improvement of various financial facilities, we should implement the work needed in the new era. The government intends to thoroughly manage facilities to stabilize the people's lives in various fields, such as autonomous management of rice, improvement of silkworm cocoons, control of fertilizers, establishment of central financial institutions for commercial and industrial associations, establishment of automobile industry, self-supply of liquid fuels, promotion of civil aviation, strengthening of maritime transport, construction of new railway lines, and protection of overseas colonial undertakings, which are all regarded as contributing to the stability of the people's lives, and attempt to establish special companies for industry and electricity etc. (6th Allied Press Telegram)

Baba's Speech on Finance 72

(Tokyo) Minister of Finance Baba gave a speech, the gist of which is as follows:

The actual budget for the eleventh year of Showa (1936) is generally based on the budget that was never established. The total amount of income and expenditure for the actual budget and the supplementary budget is more than 2,333 million yuan, which is more than 25.1 million yuan more than the budget that was never established. The actual budget is more than 1,941 million yuan, and the supplementary budget is more than 362.3 million yuan. The expenses for the supplementary budget include the Manchurian Incident expenses, expenses for improving military equipment of the army and navy, special expenses for assisting poor farmers and assisting the economic recovery of rural areas, water conservancy projects, the second horse administration plan, liquid fuel policy, establishment of financial institutions for small and medium-sized commercial industries, promotion of trade, promotion of civil aviation, expenses for promoting the northeast, expenses related to disaster relief, etc.

Secondly, for the public bonds in the eleventh year, more than 725 million yuan is for general accounting and more than 74.8 million yuan is for special accounting. Among them, more than 511.6 million yuan of the income for general accounting is used to repay public bonds. In our country, which is on the road to leap forward, the current state of its international status requires an increase in national expenditure. Estimating income and expenditure, it is necessary to consolidate the foundation of finance. It is clear that we cannot rely solely on deficit public bonds. Therefore, it is necessary to fundamentally reform the tax system, and to thoroughly review the income of monopoly businesses and other government-run businesses, as well as the income and expenditure of various special accounts, in order to increase the income of the national treasury. At this time, it is necessary to urgently seek to establish local finances, which are related to central finances. Therefore, it is necessary to implement tax system reform in order to correct the uneven burden on the people.

Deficit public bonds have been issued in a considerable amount, and will continue to be issued in the future. The reason is that the government wants to smoothly implement the public bond policy, so as to avoid the adverse effects of currency inflation on the economic world. At present, the Bank of Japan is reducing the discount on public bonds, and ordinary banks and other financial institutions are also reducing the interest rates on deposits and loans. In addition, the government's deposit department has also greatly reduced the interest rates on new and old loans, and in accordance with this purpose, it has carried out low-interest borrowing and exchange of 779 million yuan of 5% interest-bearing national treasury bonds twice. Therefore, the public bonds issued are all at a 3.5% interest rate. As for improving finance, it is necessary to reduce the financial burden on rural and fishing villages, and to smoothly implement other appropriate financial controls for small and medium-sized commercial industries and the people's finance. Although the current trade situation in our country has various obstacles from various countries, it is still able to achieve extraordinary development. Therefore, this trend must be promoted and promoted, in order to improve our country's international balance of payments and to enrich the national economic strength. Officials and merchants should work together to maintain overseas markets and strive to engage in development.

The exchange rate of the Japanese yen is still low. In the future, attention should be paid to the international movement of capital. Regarding the management of foreign exchange, it is necessary to severely crack down on it to prevent capital flight and exchange rate fluctuations. Considering the purpose of coexistence and co-prosperity between Japan and Manchuria, it is essential to ensure the smooth progress of sound investment in Manchuria. Therefore, the government has decided to give appropriate assistance to the issuance of state bonds and the issuance of corporate bonds by the South Manchuria Railway in "Manchukuo". (6th Allied Press Telegram)

Minister of the Army Terauchi Reports on the Truth of the Tokyo Incident 73

(Tokyo) Minister of the Army Terauchi explained the truth and process of the February 26th Incident in the House of Peers on the 6th. The gist is as follows:

It is extremely regrettable that an unprecedented and unfortunate incident has occurred, endangering many important national ministers. However, those who participated in the rebellious acts and those who held radical ideas were only a very small part of the entire army. The overall image of the military has not been shaken at all. The outline of the incident has been announced many times, that is, more than 1,400 officers and soldiers belonging to the 1st and 3rd Infantry Regiments, the 3rd Guards Infantry Regiment, and the 7th Field Heavy Artillery Regiment, attacked the Prime Minister's official residence, the residence of Interior Minister Saito, the residence of Education Minister Watanabe, the residence of Finance Minister Takahashi, and the residence of Grand Chamberlain Suzuki on the morning of February 26, and occupied the area around Nagatacho. There were also a small number of troops who attacked the former residence of Interior Minister Yuhara Makino. The Tokyo Garrison Commander immediately commanded the troops stationed in Tokyo to suppress the unrest and maintain order. At 3:00 p.m., a wartime security order was issued to the 1st Division's jurisdiction. A partial provision of the martial law order was implemented in Tokyo on the 27th, and at the same time, the martial law headquarters was formed. Local troops were successively ordered to come to Tokyo. At that time, it was of course possible to take strong measures to quell the rebellious troops, but because of the fear that compatriots would fight each other, causing bloodshed, and endangering nearby important institutions and important people's residences, we had to endure and restrain ourselves and earnestly advised the leaders of the rebellious troops to surrender and return. Those who participated in the incident's actions were rebellious acts, a fact that was clear when the young men left the barracks. However, at that time, they were not called rebellious troops, and were formally placed under the command of their original regimental commanders. This kind of expedient measure was also a painstaking effort to avoid stimulating the young men's excited state. However, after three days, this purpose could not be achieved, so on the 29th, we had to resolve everything by force. Fortunately, there was no exchange of fire, and it was completely quelled in the afternoon. The military authorities, in order to eliminate the root of the disaster, supervised the military and police agencies, and closely contacted the judicial police to search in various aspects. Regarding the results, because they are related to public security, the contents will be explained in a closed meeting. In the military, the absoluteness of military command and obedience is the root of military discipline. The rebellious troops' officers offended the sacredness of the order, but the lower-ranking soldiers believed that it was an order from their superiors and joined the rebellious troops. The military authorities are now making their best efforts to clarify the responsibility for the origin, command, and action of the order, so as to avoid leaving a root of disaster in the future, and to avoid causing the people to have doubts about the military service obligation. The motive of the young men's uprising was to correct and renovate the current state of the country. However, it is regrettable that the foundation of their guiding spirit was the national innovation thought that was harbored by outsiders and was absolutely incompatible with the national polity. In short, the army led by the Emperor's own troops was an unacceptable rebellious act in the current action, and it is unbearable to hate. The military is determined to self-examine, self-warn, and rectify military discipline, in order to live up to the Emperor's trust and the people's trust. (6th Allied Press Telegram)

Kwantung Army Requests Expansion of Troops Stationed in Manchuria 74

Part of the 1st Division to Depart for Manchuria Tomorrow

(Tokyo) Lieutenant General Itagaki, Chief of Staff of the Kwantung Army, and Colonel Seishi, Chief of the 1st Section, who came to Tokyo on the 30th of last month to attend the Chief of Staff Conference, have been meeting with key figures in the Central Army for days to report on the military situation in "Manchukuo," the special situation in the Soviet-Manchurian and Mongolian border areas, and the state of the Soviet Red Army's deployment in the Far East, and to propose expanding the Kwantung Army's equipment, increasing investment in Manchuria, and immigrating to Manchuria as countermeasures. They also conveyed the Kwantung Army's opinions on this issue. The opinions of the Central Army are also consistent with this, and it has been decided to increase the Kwantung Army's equipment in the next few years from Showa 12 (1937) onwards, in order to ensure that the defense of "Manchukuo" is foolproof. Colonel Sakanishi is now scheduled to return to his post alone at 3:00 p.m. on the 5th, after completing his official duties, to report all the details to Commander Ueda. According to the Kwantung Army's opinion, expanding military equipment, investing in Manchuria, and immigration policy are important matters for the national policy towards Manchuria, so the government should actively assist investment in Manchuria. Regarding the immigration issue, it is ideal to make the annual increase of Japan's population of 1 million people as immigrants to "Manchukuo." (6th Allied Press Telegram)

(Tokyo) The Ministry of the Army announced that a part of the 1st Division will depart from Shinagawa, Shibuya, Kofu and other places on May 8 to travel to Manchuria. (6th Allied Press Telegram)

Military Celebration of the Invasion of the Philippines a Success - Mussolini's Roar 75

Determined to Uphold the Acquired Victory with Great Courage

(Rome) Prime Minister Mussolini delivered a speech tonight, broadcasting to the whole country, stating that Italy's victory was a victory of civilization over barbarism, and that no country in the world could force Italy to abandon what it had conquered. The various ethnic groups in the "Black Lion" country (i.e. Abyssinia) were all convinced and happy to live and work under the Italian tricolor flag. This fact is obvious and very clear. The military officers and tribal chiefs of Abyssinia have been defeated and those who fled have fled. These people are exhausted and powerless and we need not worry about them. Looking back to October 2nd of last year, when the Italian-Abyssinian War was about to begin, I solemnly declared that I would do my best to prevent the Italian-Abyssinian War from degenerating into a European War. I deeply believe that if European peace is threatened, it will be the collapse of the entire Europe. I have fulfilled this promise. However, I must also solemnly declare that we have achieved significant victory with great courage and unwavering determination. We are now prepared to maintain victory with the same spirit and determination, lest it be lost.

The Prime Minister then expressed his condolences and gratitude to the soldiers who fought in East Africa and the workers who served in foreign lands. His concluding remarks were, "Revolutionary Black Shirt comrades, men and women compatriots across the country, our journey has now completed a stage, and we should continue to move forward with a spirit of peace, and with confidence and determination to bravely face the tasks ahead. I now shout long live Italy, may this sound reach Africa, where all soldiers can hear it! Long live Italy!" (5th Havas Telegram)

Bells and Whistles Ring Together - General Mobilization of Roman Citizens 76

(Rome) The government received a telegram this afternoon from General Badoglio, the Senior Italian Commissioner and Commander-in-Chief of the Expeditionary Force in Italian East Africa, stating, "This Commander-in-Chief has led the victorious troops into the capital of Abyssinia at 4:00 p.m. today." At 5:30 p.m., the whistles in Rome rang together, and the bells throughout the country rang to announce the general mobilization of citizens. In an instant, flags were immediately raised at the ends of houses, and all work was stopped. Fascist Party members all rushed home to change into black shirt uniforms, and within forty minutes, they gathered at designated locations. At that time, the streets were full of Fascist Party members rushing east and west. Public buses, business cars, and all other vehicles were also full of party members. Soon, only women and children remained in the vehicles, because all men, even ten-year-old children, had to participate in the general mobilization, and had already gotten out of the cars and left. At that time, there were special guards stationed in front of the British Embassy and Consulate, including many military police and soldiers, for protection. Traffic nearby was temporarily blocked. The number of guards in front of the embassies and consulates of other sanctioning countries has also been increased to prevent accidents. By 7:00 p.m., the crowds in front of the Palazzo Venezia had gathered to an unprecedented extent. Fascist groups held flags and sang patriotic songs, waiting for Prime Minister Mussolini. At 8:00 p.m., the Prime Minister came out to the balcony with General Badoglio's telegram and read it to the public, and gave a speech saying, "I now declare to the Italian people and the world that the war is over and peace has been restored. Since the start of the war, after seven months of fierce fighting, I am now able to declare this to the public. I cannot help but feel touched, and I am also proud of it. Moreover, this peace is our peace, that is, peace in the style of ancient Rome. The peace in the style of Rome can be summarized in one sentence, that is, Abyssinia belongs to Italy. This sentence is simple and clear, and it is also unwavering. I mention it here because it is absolutely necessary." Tonight, the enthusiastic rejoicing of the Italian nation is unprecedented. Fascist groups from all over the world gathered at designated locations to listen to the Prime Minister's broadcast speech (see previous telegram). (5th Havas Agency Telegram)

Italy Views Abyssinia as Forbidden Fruit 77

Claims Complete Sovereignty Should Be Enjoyed, Not Tolerating Other Countries' Interference

(Rome) It was learned today that the House will meet on the 9th of this month to pass a bill declaring Italy's complete sovereignty over Abyssinia's capital. (National Telegram, 6th)

(Rome) Semi-official sources recently explained Italy's views on the Italian army's occupation of the Abyssinian capital, stating that the Abyssinian state no longer exists, its government has been overthrown, and its unified situation has been eliminated. At this point, it is merely a part of Italian territory. Since the Abyssinian Emperor's departure, Abyssinia has had no government, and Italy can hardly consider even nominally attempting to establish a new government in the future. In the future, Italian troops may continue operations in southern Abyssinia, but their nature will be to clear out the remaining enemy and stabilize the area, which is not comparable to war. Even from the perspective of the League of Nations, Abyssinia no longer exists, so there is no need to protect it, and its mission is over. This is the general outline. As for the details, Italy is willing to consult with Britain, France, and even the League of Nations to protect various interests, but Italy refuses to discuss the legality of conquering Abyssinia under any circumstances. Since Abyssinia completely belongs to Italy, Italy will refuse any attempt to divide it in the future. Semi-official sources finally stated that Italy's outward expansion policy will not end with the conquest of Abyssinia but has only completed the first stage. (Havas, 6th)

Roman Governor Botti Appointed Governor of Abyssinia's Capital 78

(Rome) The government has recently appointed Roman Governor Botti as Governor of Abyssinia's capital. (Havas, 6th)

25,000 Italian Troops Officially Enter Abyssinia's Capital 79

All Government Offices in the City Replace with Tricolor Flags, Military Rule Reduces Terror

(London) Today, Italian troops officially entered Abyssinia's capital with flags flying and music playing, thus ending the terror in the capital. It took the Italian army seven months and three days of fighting to occupy the capital. The first person to enter the city was the Governor of Rome, Botti, leading the procession, as Botti served as an infantry officer in the army. Following him was General Badoglio, commander-in-chief of the East African Army, riding a white horse and leading a squadron of Carabinieri, followed by a regiment of grenade launchers, and then a squadron of Eritrean soldiers. Then, trucks loaded with soldiers and military supplies arrived one after another. By afternoon, 25,000 Italian soldiers had entered the city. As the Italian troops entered the city, 50 airplanes soared in the sky. (Reuters, 5th)

Abyssinia's Capital After seven months of war, the Italian army finally completely occupied Abyssinia's capital today. Italian Commander-in-Chief Badoglio ordered the city to be entered at noon today. It was led by 20 motorcycle escorts, followed by nine small tanks, and then the main force of the large Sabauda Division, traveling in many military vehicles. After that came Commander-in-Chief Badoglio, leading generals and staff members in the headquarters vehicle, with native soldiers providing cover on both sides of the road. Badoglio went directly to the Italian embassy to set up headquarters. By 4 p.m., all government offices in the city had been occupied. The Italian army's appearance was very impressive. There were very few Abyssinians along the way. The palace is now flying a single-color flag. In the evening, the Abyssinia's Capital station was also occupied by Italian engineering teams. Abyssinia's Capital is now under military rule, and the chaotic situation of the previous days has suddenly stabilized. (National Telegram, 5th)

Abyssinia's Capital The bandits and scattered soldiers in Abyssinia's Capital have stopped looting. These people have hidden their rifles, raised white flags, and cheered to welcome the Italian troops entering the city, and saluted with the Fascist salute. When Italian soldiers sang and cheered as they passed through the streets, the Abyssinians showed no signs of resistance, so not a single shot was fired. Most of the new districts of Abyssinia's Capital have become rubble fields with smoke rising everywhere. Many extremely exquisite buildings were reduced to ashes. Many shops were looted, and many houses were burned down. The streets were filled with various broken items and war relics. (Reuters, 6th)

To Seek Justice Through Diplomatic Channels

Jerusalem The Emperor of Abyssinia set sail from Djibouti, French East Africa, yesterday on a British warship to come here. It is estimated that he will arrive by the end of this week. (Havas, 6th)

Failure of Collective Action, the Fate of the League of Nations Will End 83

Calls for Reorganization are Rampant, Small Nordic Countries Consider Leaving the League

Danish Capital The fate of the League of Nations will be decided in Geneva in the next few days. It is rumored that the foreign authorities of Norway, Finland, Sweden, Denmark, and the Netherlands will meet in Geneva on Saturday and Sunday to consider the issue of withdrawing from the League of Nations. It is rumored that Switzerland and Spain will also join the meeting later to make a final decision on this issue. (Reuters, 6th)

(London) According to political figures, the British government is now considering proposing a reorganization of the League of Nations because the League of Nations' handling of the Italian-Abyssinian dispute has failed. The method is no more than the following two points: 1. Divide the League of Nations Covenant and the Treaty of Versailles into two. 2. Mutual assistance obligations should be designated to regions and no longer have universal characteristics. The method is to divide the countries of the world into several regions. Countries participating in a mutual assistance convention in a certain region bear the obligation of immediate military mutual assistance within that region, while countries belonging to other regional conventions only provide advisory opinions. Some political figures believe that once the above reorganization method is realized, the constraints borne by Britain will only be limited to Western Europe. It is rumored that the British government has not yet made a decision on the reorganization issue and will study it in the long term after the Italian-Abyssinian issue is truly resolved. (Havas, 5th)

(London) People seem to be more interested in the future of the League of Nations. Letters to newspapers discussing this issue are endless. Most people consider the possibility of improving the League of Nations to avoid its demise. Lord Lothian also sent a letter to The Times, advocating the deletion of Articles 10 and 16 of the League of Nations Covenant, saying that this move could enable the League of Nations to use great power to seek peace, because there is no threat after the mediation proposal. The Daily Telegraph praised Prime Minister Baldwin's reply to the British League of Nations Association delegation: "We must clarify the position of the League of Nations." The British League of Nations Association plans to hold a general meeting at Albert Hall on Friday to proceed with its proposal to continue sanctions against Italy. (Reuters, 6th)

(London) The Italian war in East Africa is now over. How about the future of the League of Nations and Abyssinia? All the world's capitals and newspapers have various speculations about it.

Italian Prime Minister Expresses No Desire to Hinder British Interests 84

Willing to Establish Authority Throughout Abyssinia, Absolutely No Intention of Coveting Egypt

(London) Italian Prime Minister Mussolini recently made an important speech to Mr. Price, a special reporter for the Daily Mail, explaining that Italy's policy has absolutely no intention of hindering Britain. The purpose of this speech is to extend a hand of friendship to Britain. He said, "The Italian government has absolutely no intention of coveting Egypt. As far as I am concerned, Egypt is an independent country in the Mediterranean and not a country on the African continent. Italy and Egypt have always had a good friendship, and we should maintain friendly relations in the future. As for Anglo-Egyptian Sudan and Palestine, Italy has no political interests in these places." The Prime Minister then said, "Italy's wishes in terms of colonies have been satisfied after the conquest of Abyssinia. In the future, Italy can be among the 'satisfied' countries." Referring to the Abyssinian peace issue, the Prime Minister said, "For the benefit of all related countries, it seems most appropriate for Italian authority to be quickly established within Abyssinia. As for the terms of peace, they should be based on the spirit of ancient Rome and should not come out of a malformed peace. We advocate that the Abyssinian issue must be resolved once and for all, because the sacrifices, bloodshed, and money we have made for Abyssinia are all borne independently, without relying on others. The solution to the Abyssinian issue should take this into account. However, if Italy's friendly countries are engaged in economic enterprises in Abyssinia, we will definitely not close the door to them." At this point, Price asked whether the so-called friendly countries included Britain, France, and other sanctioning countries. The Prime Minister replied, "Yes." He also said, "Once the countries of the world learn about our country's true financial strength, they will be surprised, just like they learned about the truth of our military strength. The discussion of the reorganization of the League of Nations is now urgent. Italy is ready to come out to help. I personally think that the League of Nations can continue to exist, or even needs to exist. However, the responsibilities it bears should be commensurate with its power, and the spirit of the League of Nations Covenant should be adapted to the needs of various countries and the situation in European countries." Referring to the Rhine River issue, the Prime Minister said, "After the German army entered the Rhine River area, Italy adopted an absolutely reserved attitude because the sanctions were still in the implementation period. Italy is now ready to help, so that the major countries of Western Europe can establish sincere and practical understanding, because these countries must eventually reach an agreement, otherwise, once the war starts, the result will be the complete overthrow of the entire European culture." (Havas, 5th)

Japanese Army in North China Expanding a Division 86

Applying Wartime Establishment with 16,000 Personnel, Barracks Being Built in Tianjin, Qin, Chang, Tang

Tianjin Correspondence: The strengthening of the Japanese garrison in North China has recently been decided. Originally, the Japanese military planned to dispatch 5,000 elite soldiers from the 1st, 3rd, 4th, and 8th Divisions from within the country, in addition to the 2,800 infantry and artillery troops currently stationed there, and form a mixed brigade, still stationed along the Peining Railway line and the special areas of Tianjin and Beijing in accordance with the Boxer Protocol. Unexpectedly, last month, the Chief of Staff of the Japanese Army stationed in Tianjin, Nagami, returned to Japan to attend the Division Commander's Meeting, bringing with him a proposal from the Japanese Commander Tada Shun, stating how important the situation in North China was and how urgent the anti-communist military affairs were. In order to protect all Japanese rights and interests in North China and the safety of overseas Chinese, it was necessary to expand the military strength to more than one division in order to provide thorough protection. At this time, Tada was still at the rank of Major General, and with the expansion of military strength, he hoped to continue to serve as commander, and at the same time, he could be promoted by one rank, so the wording was deliberately sensational. The proposal was actually passed and obtained the promise of the Japanese military, so the original intention was changed. After Nagami returned to Tianjin, he prepared a budget and sent Senior Staff Officer Ishii back to Tokyo, and presented it to the Japanese military when attending the Chief of Staff's Meeting. There is no problem in implementation. The number of soldiers in this division is 12,000 to 16,000, fully adopting the wartime establishment. The system is the same as that of the Japanese garrison in Taiwan. All mechanized, chemical, air-land tank, and special forces are included. In addition to the troops currently stationed there, the newly added soldiers should be around 13,000. Although the name is a division, the strength exceeds 20,000 people. They will still be selected from the elite troops stationed in Hiroshima, Utsunomiya, Tokyo, and Hokkaido. Not a single unit will be dispatched separately to avoid weak strength. The first batch of troops is scheduled to depart from Tokyo in early June and arrive in North China in mid-June. They will continue to arrive one after another and can complete the expansion by the end of June. At present, the Japanese military is rushing to prepare barracks. 700 new barracks are being built in the Limingzhuang area of Dongjuzi in Tianjin, divided into 27 places. Only bricks and tiles require more than 50 million cubic feet. The construction cost is 400,000 yuan. More than 1,300 Chinese and foreign workers are being gathered to rush the construction. About the end of June, a part can be completed. The occupied land belongs to Li Chun, the former Soviet Governor, and the Peining Railway Bureau. Although they promised to give a price, they have not paid a penny so far. There are also more than 40 acres of private land (the barracks occupy a total of 1,340 acres) that have also been occupied. In the future, negotiations will lead to the best outcome, and perhaps a lower price will be paid. In the Japanese concession, the building of the Xilai Hotel on Mingishi Street, with about 200 rooms, and the Gongli Hospital on Fukushima Street, with 100 rooms, have also been occupied by the Japanese military and are being repaired. They are planned to be used as garrisons for special forces. In addition, one barracks each will be found along the Peining Line in places such as Luanxian, Changli, and Liushouying. In Qinhuangdao, Nandasi, and Tangshan, new houses are being built next to the old barracks. All are limited to be completed next month. However, the purpose of the Japanese military to increase its troops is not to equip a strong force in eastern Hebei, but to enter and exit the Pinghan and Jinpu lines. Recently, the Japanese side has already expressed its intention in the diplomatic negotiations in Hebei and Chahar, requesting to station Japanese troops in Fengtai. A number of Japanese troops will also be stationed in Changxindian, Baoding, and Shijiazhuang on the Pinghan Road, and Yangliuqing, Jinghai, and Botouzhen on the Jinpu Line, saying that they are assisting in anti-communism. The authorities have not yet allowed this. However, with such a large increase in Japanese troops, it is impossible not to find a suitable garrison. Therefore, in the future, the stationing of troops in the above areas will still be impossible to reject. As for the newly appointed commander of the Japanese garrison in North China, Wanyilang Tashiro, he will arrive around June 15. Tada will return home around the 20th after handing over his post. Tashiro is a current division commander and one of the few China experts. He served as the Major General Chief of Staff of the Ueda Division in the Shanghai War. As for his experience, he is from Saga Prefecture and graduated from the 15th class of the Military Academy. In 1904, he was appointed as a second lieutenant of infantry, and graduated from the Army University. He served as the Chief of the China Section of the General Staff Headquarters, the Commander of the 28th Infantry Brigade, a military attache in China, the Chief of Staff of the Shanghai Expeditionary Army, and the Commander of the Kwantung Army Gendarmerie. In August 1934, he was appointed as the Commander of the Gendarmerie. In September 1935, he was appointed as the Commander of the 11th Division. He was awarded the fifth class merit for his meritorious service in the Russo-Japanese War. He was awarded the Order of the Rising Sun, Double Rays, Third Class Merit for his meritorious service in the Northeast and Shanghai wars. (5th)

The Truth About the Monetary Famine in Sichuan Province 87

Due to Manipulation by Unscrupulous Merchants, Copper Coins are Lacking, People of Sichuan Hope for New Subsidiary Coins to be Shipped to Sichuan for Relief

Chengdu Correspondence: The huge quantity, complex types, poor quality, and disparate prices of copper coins in Sichuan Province are unique in the history of coinage, both ancient and modern, Chinese and foreign. From the second year of the Republic of China to the seventeenth year, a situation of copper coins flooding the market gradually formed. Subsidiary coins became worse and worse, and prices became more and more expensive. In the seventeenth year, due to the disputes over factory-made, mixed-plate, half-dollar and large-dollar silver coins, copper coins were temporarily valued by people. From the eighteenth year to the twenty-third and fourth years, the silver coin problem was resolved, and then a large number of copper coins suddenly appeared on the market. In the spring and summer seasons of the twenty-fourth year, one silver coin could be exchanged for 30,000 copper coins (that is, 150 pieces of 200-wen copper coins). Sichuan Province is not short of copper coins, which can be used as solid evidence. However, since the implementation of the new currency system, ordinary villagers have become accustomed to using hard coins and have gradually valued copper coins again. In addition, unscrupulous merchants have spread rumors and manipulated them, creating several different exchange rates in Chengdu and Chongqing and in various counties, using copper as currency to profit back and forth, which has led to the phenomenon of the current monetary famine in Chengdu. Since the 27th and 28th of last month, copper coins have almost disappeared from the Chengdu market. All money shops have removed their exchange rate signs and do not accept one-jiao legal tender. The silver and money general market in Anle Temple on Shuncheng Street has been closed for several days. As a result, public officials and those who pull carts and sell drinks are feeling great hardship. According to reliable investigations, copper coins (referring to the copper coins minted in Sichuan Province over the years) are not lacking in Chengdu and various counties. It is only because the value of legal tender has fallen due to rumors spread by unscrupulous merchants. All merchants and civilians who receive copper coins are unwilling to transport copper to the market and exchange them for legal tender. This is the crux of the monetary famine in Chengdu. According to Zhang Shaoquan, who used to work at the Chengdu Mint, the types and numbers of copper coins minted by the factory over the years have been found. A list is specially attached below. From this, a conclusion can be drawn: The number of small 200-wen copper coins currently circulating in Sichuan Province is at least 600 million pieces (including privately minted ones). In addition, the number of large 200-wen, 100-wen, and 50-wen copper coins is no less than 1 billion pieces. It is extremely contradictory that such a huge amount is suffering from a monetary famine. At this moment, knowledgeable people in Sichuan Province unanimously hope that the central government will quickly ship new subsidiary coins to Sichuan for relief. If they cannot be minted in time, various old copper coins can be temporarily allowed to circulate by discounting their prices according to their quality. After a certain period of time, they should be collected and destroyed as waste copper and strictly prohibited from being used, as a temporary solution. The types and numbers of copper coins minted by the Chengdu Mint from the second year of the Republic of China to the seventeenth year are listed below.

The above list shows the numbers reported by the factory. As for the coins privately minted during the garrison era of various military factions, there are no accurate statistics. (May 3rd)

Anhui, Jiangxi, and Zhejiang Discuss Joint Control and Marketing of Green Tea 88

Zhejiang Province sends personnel to investigate the sales situation; a total of two million yuan is needed for loans and relief; Liu Zhenhua writes to Huang Shaohong to request his leadership.

Hangzhou Correspondence: Zhejiang is an important tea-producing province, especially known overseas for its Pingshui green tea, which is welcomed in European and American markets. According to a survey by the Zhejiang Economic Investigation Institute of the Central Construction Committee, tea is produced in 63 counties within the nine old prefectures of Shao, Hang, Yan, Chu, Jin, Wen, Qu, Hu, and Ning. The total annual output is 318,474 dan, of which the seven counties under the Shao prefecture (namely the Pingshui area) produce the most, estimated at over 100,000 dan. Approximately 200,000 boxes are exported annually, each box containing 50 catties, with a value of about 10 million yuan based on 80 yuan per dan. Recently, due to the control and marketing of black tea in Shanghai by Anhui and Jiangxi provinces, tea merchants in Shanghai have implemented a suspension of foreign exchange bills to show their opposition, leading to a shortage of funds for tea merchants in various places to purchase tea. As new tea from Zhejiang Province is currently entering the market, tea prices have plummeted as a result, causing great panic among tea farmers. The Anhui provincial government believes that since Anhui and Jiangxi provinces have already provided loans and relief for black tea, and counties such as Xiuning and Shexian in Anhui Province, as well as Wuyuan County in Jiangxi Province, also produce large quantities of green tea, with annual exports of about 100,000 boxes, only one-third of Zhejiang Province's output. Therefore, they intend to further unite with Zhejiang and Jiangxi provinces to continue providing loans to tea merchants and implement joint control and marketing of green tea for thorough relief. Anhui Construction Department Secretary Chen Yan was specially dispatched, carrying a personal letter from Liu Zhenhua, to visit Zhejiang Provincial Chairman Huang Shaohong, Civil Affairs Department Director Xu Qingfu, and Construction Department Director Wu Tingyang, among others, to explain the process of Anhui and Jiangxi's joint control and marketing of black tea, the opposition of tea merchants to the suspension of foreign exchange bills, and future opinions on uniting Zhejiang, Anhui, and Jiangxi provinces to control and market tea to relieve tea farmers, or to establish a new marketing organization led by Zhejiang Province. Huang, Xu, Wu, and others all expressed deep sympathy. However, Zhejiang Province must first conduct a detailed investigation into the production and sales of Pingshui green tea. Wu Tingyang convened relevant personnel from the Construction Department for a discussion. Although the required bank loan is estimated to be around two million yuan, Xu Qingfu can negotiate with the Farmers Bank of China for a loan, which should not be a problem. It was decided to send Zhu Huiging, Director of the Bureau of Commerce and Industry, to Shanghai today (the 5th) to investigate the sales situation of Pingshui green tea. Regarding fundamental solutions, a Pingshui Tea Industry Improvement Center will be established to guide tea farmers in all aspects of improved cultivation and tea-making methods. An application has been submitted to the National Economic Commission for an appropriation of funds to subsidize the expenses, and concrete measures have been discussed for cooperation with Zhejiang Province for improvement. The commission has agreed to allocate 14,000 yuan for the establishment of the improvement center. Currently, the site urgently needs to be determined, and the Rice and Wheat Field Director Mo Dingsen, tea expert Wu Juenong, technician Lu Yunfu, and others have been dispatched again to cross the river to Shaoxing Shengxian on the morning of the 5th to re-survey the location for setting up the improvement center. (May 5th)

Guangdong Province Encourages the Establishment of Shipping Routes to Southeast Asia 89

The Construction Department drafts measures pending verification and implementation; approval for five years of exclusive navigation and provision of subsidies.

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Guangdong provincial authorities have vigorously promoted shipping administration and construction in recent years. In the first three-year plan for shipping construction in the province, it was decided to first complete the province's shipping route network and then establish routes to other ports. However, in Southeast Asia, due to the large number of overseas Chinese, passenger and cargo traffic has relied on foreign commercial vessels. The local overseas Chinese, mostly from Fujian and Guangdong provinces, are eager for the provincial government to quickly complete direct shipping routes between Guangzhou and Southeast Asia, in order to recover outflowing profits. Currently, Ding Peilong, Director of the Guangzhou Port Authority, has adopted the opinion of Cui Longwen, a resident of Nanhai County, to expedite the establishment of commercial vessel direct routes to various Southeast Asian ports, and has submitted it to the Construction Department for deliberation and implementation. The opinion believes that the key to implementing shipping operations is capital. If the government finds it difficult to raise funds temporarily, it can encourage the people with various conveniences to demonstrate its promotion. Overseas Chinese in various ports are known for their patriotic enthusiasm and should be able to actively raise shares to operate the shipping business. After review, the Construction Department believes that it can be adopted and has immediately drafted measures to submit to the provincial government for implementation. The measures are as follows: Announce rewards to the people for revitalizing the shipping industry, especially focusing on overseas Chinese, so that they can raise funds themselves to operate shipping routes to Southeast Asia. The reward measures are divided into two items: (A) Approval for five years of exclusive navigation. (B) From the date of commencement of navigation until the end of the five-year exclusive navigation period, the government will issue subsidies annually, tentatively set at 35% of the ship's management expenses. The service measures are divided into six items: (A) Vessels receiving government subsidies should be subject to government command and use in case of national emergencies. The amount of supplementary payment during the period of use will be determined separately. (B) Responsible for carrying mail; detailed rules for freight charges will be formulated separately. (C) The government will send a number of navigation and machinery trainees to serve and practice on board. (D) Without government permission, the vessel shall not be transferred or sold to foreigners. (E) When repairing, repair at domestic government or merchant-operated shipyards as far as possible. (F) Passenger and cargo fares must be submitted to the government for approval and shall not be increased or decreased without authorization. (May 2nd)

Burial ceremony held after the memorial service; the burial site is in Zuojialong with excellent scenery.

Changsha Correspondence: After Mr. Ding Wenjiang passed away in Changsha on January 3rd of this year due to coal gas poisoning, the entire country mourned, considering it a significant loss to the academic community. Therefore, when the memorial service was held at the Changsha Yinying Palace on May 3rd, although the ceremony and layout all followed Mr. Ding's will, striving for simplicity and plainness, important figures and scholars from home and abroad all came to pay their respects. The chief officiant was Weng Wenhao, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, along with Chairman He Jian of Hunan Province, in plain attire and white horses, showing extreme sorrow. On the 4th, the coffin was exhumed and buried in Zuojialong, Yuelu Mountain. The scenery there is excellent. From now on, the scholar's remains will forever accompany the famous mountain, and his spirit will be immortal. (May 5th)
