Fire Drill Conducted by Various Fire Brigades and Police in Nanshi Yesterday 133

At 3:00 PM, Bombs Exploded in Lujiabang, Starting a Fire; More Than Ten Fire Trucks Extinguished it in Twenty Minutes

In order to promote public awareness of disaster prevention, various Nanshi agencies held a fire drill at the intersection of Lujiabang Road and Xieqiao Road in Nanshi at 3:00 PM yesterday. Assuming that at 3:00 PM, the incident location was bombed and caught fire, the fire brigades of the east, south, west, and north districts of the city immediately dispatched more than ten fire trucks to rush to the rescue. The Traffic Division, Inspection Department, Ximen Branch, and nearby Tenth Precinct of the Municipal Public Security Bureau all sent personnel to the scene to maintain traffic. The ambulances of the Sanitation Team rescued the injured from the fire in the raging flames. Thirty or forty members of the 4th, 6th, 7th, and 8th teams of the South Shanghai District Defense Corps, who lived near Lujiabang Road, all came to participate and maintain order without prior arrangement. The fire was extinguished in less than twenty minutes, and the scene was realistic. The Huadong News Agency reporter recorded the drill as follows:

Thatched Sheds Built in Advance; The Municipal Public Security Bureau built a thatched shed in the shape of a three-dimensional high-rise building at the intersection of Lujiabang Road and Xieqiao Road starting at 7:00 AM yesterday. It was made of bamboo and thatch, but the public was not notified in advance. At 2:00 PM, the fire brigades of the South Shanghai District were notified to gather at a certain place upon receiving a phone call at 2:00 PM. At 2:30 PM, Huang Tizhi, the acting director of the Ximen Branch, led the members of each precinct to maintain traffic at the scene. Tens of thousands of citizens considered it a spectacle and stood on the streets. Some even surrounded the rooftops, waiting for the disaster to come. The number of people exceeded 20,000.

A Loud Bang, a Bomb Exploded, and a Fire Started; At 3:00 PM, the police at a certain location on Lujiabang Road and Xieqiao Road suddenly heard a loud bang, and the location was set on fire as a simulation. They immediately reported it to the Ximen Branch by phone, which was relayed to the headquarters. Cai Jinjun, the director of the Public Security Bureau, immediately dispatched Inspector Dong Guangfu, Director Wu Fengwen of the Fire Prevention Division, and Luo Deming, a member of the Traffic Division, to the scene. The South Shanghai District Fire Brigade Joint Association also received the fire alarm phone call.

Fire Trucks Arrived Within Two Minutes; Xia Guoliang, the commander-in-chief of the South Shanghai District and the director of the Southwest District of South Shanghai, received the phone call and immediately dispatched three fire trucks from the Southwest District to the incident location on Xieqiao and Lujiabang Roads. He also telegraphed He Yongshou, the director of the Southeast District Fire Brigade of South Shanghai, Zhu Kuangshi, the director of the South District Fire Brigade of South Shanghai, Lu Jinlin, the director of the North District Fire Brigade of South Shanghai, and the Dongjiadu Fire Brigade of the Second District, etc. Within two minutes, more than ten fire trucks from each district arrived together.

Rescuing the Injured from the Fire; Each fire brigade, in the order of their arrival, found fire hydrants near the two ends of Xieqiao Road and the middle section of Lujiabang Road and aimed at the incident location to pour water. The fire trucks at the forefront also raised high-rise ladders and poured water from above. More than ten fire trucks fired from near and far, extinguishing the fire within five minutes. Many men and women who were burned by the fire were rescued from the houses inside the fire, and the Sanitation Team rescued them with swift means and wrapped them up well in the ambulances.

Completely Extinguished in Twenty Minutes; At that time, the Municipal Public Security Bureau Inspection Department, Fire Prevention Division, Traffic Division, Ximen Branch, and all precinct stations were at the scene to maintain traffic order, so there was no looting during the fire. More than 30 members of the 4th, 6th, 7th, and 8th teams of the South Shanghai District Defense Corps, who lived near Xieqiao Road in Lujiabang, also automatically participated in maintaining order. Therefore, under the joint efforts of all parties to maintain strict prevention, the fire was completely extinguished in less than twenty minutes, at 3:20 PM.

Realistic Scene, Satisfactory Results; During the drill, the residents on both sides relied on the guidance and maintenance of the police of the Public Security Bureau, and the order was very good. The scene was realistic. After the drill, the members of each district fire brigade also listened to the instructions of the Director of the Inspection Department of the Public Security Bureau and the directors of the Fire Prevention and Traffic Divisions, and recognized that the disaster prevention actions of each district fire brigade were rapid, and that they could also cope with any eventuality. The results were very satisfactory, and the citizens who participated in the disaster prevention were instilled with the meaning of disaster prevention. At about 4:00 PM, the mock play ended.

The Qingpu-Shanghai long-distance bus company between Shanghai and Qingpu has been operating on a trial basis since February 28th. Hard Life; Leatherworker Castrates Himself in Resentment 135

Zhao Han, a native of Zhejiang, lives in a shack on Qingyun Road, Zhabei, in this city, and has been working as a leatherworker. However, he has been unlucky and has suffered repeated setbacks. Until recently, he had no business at all and often had no food. Out of desperation, he went to a temple in Zhabei, intending to shave his head and become a monk, but he was rejected by the temple and returned dejectedly. However, he had no way to make a living for the time being, and he was about to sit and wait for death. In his anxiety, he could not help but feel resentment. At about 11:00 AM yesterday, he privately cut off his genitals with a leather knife in the shack, hoping to kill himself. However, he did not die immediately and instead felt unbearable pain, crying out loudly and alarming his neighbors, who rushed to see what was happening. They then learned the whole story and reported it to the police, who hired a car to take him to the hospital for treatment. His condition is very critical, and it is very pitiful.

Xue Zhenyi's Private Prosecution: Trial of Zhao Guangfu's Case 136

Zhao Firmly Claims Xue Planned Extortion; Court Orders Retrieval of Case Files for Further Inquiry

Xue Zhenyi from Xuzhou, aged 31, was arrested in April of the 21st year of the Republic of China for attempted murder of Hai Zongqi, residing at No. 111 Pushi Road. He was found guilty by the Special Second Court and sentenced to seven years imprisonment. During the trial in the Tang Jiapeng assassination case last year, the convict Zhao Guangfu reported that Wang Xinggao and Gu Zhuxuan had incited murder. When Gu appealed to the High Court, Zhao testified that Xue Zhenyi, a prison lawyer, and Zhu Jincheng, among others, had planned to extort money from Gu. Now, Xue has been released on parole. Based on Zhao's testimony on October 2nd of the 23rd year, he believes Zhao deliberately damaged his reputation. He hired a lawyer and filed a private prosecution with the Criminal Division of the Special Second Court. Yesterday at 9 AM, Judge Chen Pusheng presided over the trial in the Second Criminal Court. The defendant, Zhao Guangfu, was brought from prison. First, the plaintiff, Xue Zhenyi, presented the grounds for his private prosecution, including a civil claim stating that Zhao was in prison in October of the 23rd year, and he, Xue, was in Ward 3 of the detention center. They fundamentally had no opportunity to meet, so how could he have planned extortion? He requested that detention center personnel be summoned to investigate. Zhao Guangfu testified that it was Xue who planned to obtain money through fraud and share it with everyone, and that he (Zhao) wrote the indictment on Xue's behalf. He claimed that Xue's status as a prison lawyer was known to all inmates, and he asked for veteran inmates to be interrogated. He claimed to have forgotten what he had previously testified in court. The court, upon reviewing the testimony, ordered the retrieval of case files for investigation and summoning of witnesses for interrogation. The next hearing was scheduled for the morning of the 13th, and Zhao was returned to prison.

Another Accusation: Ni Yueqiu Accused of Killing Three 137

Ministry of Justice Re-Assigns Case for Trial; Ni Claims He Had No Authority at the Time

Ni Yueqiu, the district chief of the Fifth District of Qilin Town in Haimen and concurrently the head of the local defense corps, took matters into his own hands when the communists spread in the 19th year of the Republic. His former teacher, Sun Yuanfu, publicly reprimanded him, incurring his wrath and leading to Sun's execution under the guise of authority. Sun's widow, Madam Sun Chen, filed accusations with the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Justice and Administration, also accusing Ni of assisting the former Haimen County Magistrate Wu Yaochun in bribery. The case was transferred to the Jiangsu High Court, which instructed the Shanghai District Court to handle it. In April of the 23rd year of the Republic, Ni Yueqiu was apprehended and tried in Nantong. As a result, Ni Yueqiu was found guilty of murder and sentenced to 16 years imprisonment. While the case was under appeal, farmers Yuan Sanlang, Yuan Shen, Yu Jianglang, and Ge Zhao, among others, jointly filed a petition with the Ministry of Justice, accusing Ni Yueqiu of using his authority to commit murder. The Ministry ordered the Shanghai District Court to handle the cases together. After an investigation by the prosecutor, a clear case was established, and another indictment was filed. Yesterday at 10 AM, Judge Chen continued the trial. Yuan Sanlang, Yuan Shen, Yu Jianglang, and Ge Zhao, among others, appeared in court, testifying that the defendant served as the district chief of the Fifth District and the head of the defense corps in Haimen County during the 19th year. At that time, due to communist disturbances in the countryside, the defendant, on July 20th of that year, personally led several members of the defense corps, under the pretext of arresting bandits, falsely accused farmers Yuan Erlang, Yuan Qinglang, Yu Jiangcai, and Ge Linggou, who had previous grudges with him, of being bandits. Without presenting them to the county for trial, he arbitrarily had them tied up and executed in the wilderness of Qilin Town. The deceased died with grievances, and the living were heartbroken, so they requested legal action. Questioned about this, Ni Yueqiu claimed that he heard the public security team had captured and executed four bandits. As district chief, he was merely an intermediary between the district and the county government and had no authority to manage judicial matters. He claimed they were instigated by others to make false accusations. The judge ordered a debate and then announced the conclusion of the trial, with a verdict scheduled for the 12th of this month.

Police Search All Night, Crack Down on Bandit Den in Jiangwan 138

Eleven Male and Female Bandit Suspects Arrested

Abbot Miao Yong of the Guanyin Temple in Gongxing Bridge North, Xibinxing Road, Zhabei, a Sichuan native aged 35, had accumulated some savings, attracting the attention of bandits. Around 1 AM on March 31st, a large group of over ten bandits, all dressed in blue cloth shirts and pants and armed with one handgun and three or four sharp knives, demolished the bamboo fence and entered through the back door. They cut the wires, pried open the doors, displayed their weapons, and forbade anyone from making a sound. First, they tied up Abbot Miao Yong with ropes and rummaged through the boxes and chests, looting the clothing and valuables of the dharma masters Jiru, Yide, Zhineng, Nengjin, and Miao Yong, worth four to five hundred yuan. The bandits escaped with their loot and disappeared. The victim, Miao Yong, reported the case to the North Station Branch Bureau, requesting an investigation. The day before yesterday, Detective Jiao Bingyun received a tip that the major robber bandits who looted the Guanyin Temple and the monk's property were hiding in the Liangjia Tomb Mountain and Gujiazhai areas of Jiangwan, requesting an investigation. He reported this to Liang Fuchu, the chief of the North Station Branch Bureau, and Gu Liancheng and Guo Mengqu, the leaders of the Detective Squad, who then reported to Cai Jingjun, the Director-General, and Zhang Datong, the Commander-in-Chief, for approval. Squad leader Gao Song and Hu Kui Sheng were dispatched, leading detectives Jiao Bingyun, Yang Fuchen, Zhang Dalong, Zhou Jitang, Kong Rongsheng, Huai Xinmao, Chen Mian, Zhang Liangjin, Yang Hanzhang, Hu Daoxi, and other personnel on duty, along with informants. They disguised themselves and, together with police officers Qu Shixin and Sun Jiyuan from the Jiangwan Police Station, rushed to the bandit den at No. 1 Liangjia Tomb Mountain around 3 AM yesterday morning. They surrounded the place. Ji Chengyu (aka Little Black Skin, a 36-year-old from Nantong), a bandit inside the house, noticed the detectives and opened fire. The bullet flew over Squad Leader Guo's head. Squad Leader Gu and Detective Jiao fearlessly charged in from the front and back. They saw Ji trying to crawl on the ground, attempting to escape through the window. They apprehended him, seized a 6-inch Browning handgun, serial number 152665, with eight bullets in the magazine, one of which was chambered but did not detonate. They found forty bullets and a spent cartridge in a newspaper-wrapped mechanism on the wall, along with a rifle butt and two magazines. Ji's wife, Zhao (a 28-year-old from Nantong), and Gu Fengxi (a 55-year-old from Haimen) were also arrested. The team interrogated them thoroughly. Ji confessed the whereabouts of his accomplices. The original team of detectives continued to Gujiazhai to arrest Ji Dahong (a 33-year-old from Nantong), Cao Zhigao (a 26-year-old from Nantong), and Bao Wenming (a 38-year-old from Nantong). Later, in Xiaogujiazhai, they arrested Yang Defu (a 29-year-old from Haimen). Then, at No. 12 Qu, Gongxing Bridge, they arrested Ge Defu (a 35-year-old from Nantong) and Lu Haitao (a 36-year-old from Nantong). Finally, they rushed to a northern-style house in Dijia浜, Yinxianggang, and arrested Zhao Jinwen (a 26-year-old from Nantong) and Cao Yonggao (a 25-year-old from Nantong). After searching all night, the detectives arrested a total of eleven male and female bandits. After detailed interrogation by Squad Leaders Gu and Guo, Ji and the others confessed to the robbery of the Guanyin Temple on Xibaoxing Road, Gongxing Bridge North, late on the night of March 31st, and the property of the monks. Because the case involved armed robbery, the North Station Branch Bureau detained them pending transfer to the General Bureau for further investigation.

Robber Shot Dead at Yuegui Lane, Identities Confirmed 139

Robber Liu Yonghua Admits to Robbery

The Caoxiangtai cotton cloth store at No. 276 Fada Road was invaded by two armed robbers at 7:50 PM the night before last. They stole eleven yuan and fled. The owner called the police, and Hua constable No. 824 from the French Concession police pursued them to Yuegui Lane on Fujian Road in the Public Concession, where he shot and killed robber Jia Guizhang (29 years old, from Shandong) and seized a handgun. The other robber, Liu Yonghua (42 years old, from Shandong), fled into No. 4 Dongxin Lane on Maidie'an Road, where Hua constable No. 220 pursued and apprehended him. He was taken back to the police station for investigation. This was reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now known that the Public Concession police transported the robber's body to the autopsy office on Feilun Road that night. Four yuan in banknotes, 41 cents, and 6 dimes were found on the deceased. The seized handgun and spent cartridges were examined and found to be linked to a previous murder. The Public Concession police also determined that the arrested robber, Liu Yonghua, had been sentenced to four years and six months imprisonment in the Public Concession Court on August 16, 1930, for robbery. Yesterday morning, the Public Concession police first reported to the Special First Court and dispatched personnel to examine the robber's body. The French Concession police then notified the Tongren Auxiliary Burial Hall to send workers to the Feilun Road autopsy office to transport Jia Guizhang's body back to the French Concession autopsy office. At noon, they reported to the Special Second Court, which appointed Prosecutor Wang Ren and a clerk to conduct the autopsy. The autopsy confirmed that the robber had been shot twice, in the head and right foot, and died from his injuries. The Tongren Auxiliary Burial Hall was ordered to bury the body. At 3 PM, the French Concession police sent the arrested robber, Liu Yonghua, to the Special Second Court. Judge Zhang Chaozuo presided over the trial in the First Criminal Court. Attorney Fei Xizhen, representing the French Police Bureau, stated the case and requested an adjournment for further investigation before requesting a trial. Detective Zuo Qihong then reported the details of the case and presented the seized handgun and stolen money. Chen Wenda, an apprentice at Caoxiangtai, and Hua constables No. 824 and No. 220, testified about the robbery and the pursuit and killing of the robber. When questioned, Liu Yonghua confessed that he met Jia Guizhang in Qingdao and came to Shanghai three days ago. They planned to rob together, but he claimed he did not carry a handgun during the robbery. The court, after reviewing the testimony, ordered an adjournment to the morning of the 13th for further inquiry. The defendant was remanded in custody.

Xu Qizhong Accused of Wastefulness: Trial Concluded 140

Verdict Scheduled for Afternoon of the 12th

Xu Qizhong, the son of the wealthy Wuxing merchant Xu Wan, living in Shanghai, filed for bankruptcy with the First Special District Court after squandering his wealth, accumulating tens of thousands in debt, and being unable to repay it. His creditors, including the Sincere Company and several others, argued that Xu's bankruptcy was solely due to wastefulness and should not be equated with bankruptcy due to business failure. Therefore, they hired attorney Le Junwei to file a criminal lawsuit against Xu based on Articles 154 and 156 of the Bankruptcy Law promulgated on October 1st of last year, requesting punishment according to the law. The court summoned Xu for trial, and Xu also hired an attorney to defend him, claiming that all debts were incurred before the implementation of the Bankruptcy Law, and the law should not be applied retroactively, arguing that ignorance is no excuse. However, this argument was strongly opposed by the plaintiff. The plaintiff's attorney continued to submit a written statement to the court after the last hearing, attacking the defendant's defense, stating that the defendant's invocation of the principle of non-retroactivity in Article 1 of the Criminal Law was a misunderstanding. The crime under the Bankruptcy Law, is conditional on the confirmation of the bankruptcy declaration as the basis for punishment. If the debtor only engages in wasteful behavior without declaring bankruptcy, there is legally no crime. The crime can only be established and punished according to law after bankruptcy is declared and confirmed. Although the defendant's wasteful behavior occurred before the implementation of the Bankruptcy Law, the bankruptcy declaration and its confirmation occurred after the implementation. Therefore, there is no room for the application of Article 1 of the Criminal Law. If the wasteful behavior and the declaration and confirmation of bankruptcy had all been completed before the implementation of the Bankruptcy Law, the defendant's defense invoking Article 1 of the Criminal Law would not be unreasonable. Since Xu Qizhong's bankruptcy occurred after the implementation of the Bankruptcy Law, even though the wasteful behavior occurred before the implementation, according to legal principles, how can he invoke that article for defense? He should be sentenced according to the law. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Tan continued to summon the defendant to the court for investigation. Attorney Le reiterated the above points and presented bills from the St. Anna and Paramount dance halls after October 1st of last year, proving that the defendant continued to waste money even after the implementation of the Bankruptcy Law. Xu's attorney defended him, emphasizing the principle of "non-retroactivity" in the Criminal Law, arguing that this was a fundamental principle of law and could not be easily overturned. The Bankruptcy Law also only sanctions crimes committed after its implementation. Xu Qizhong's wasteful behavior all occurred before the law came into effect, so he requested that the defendant be declared not guilty. Judge Tan, after the closing arguments, scheduled the verdict for the afternoon of May 12th.

Life is Hard: Wife Unsettled 141

Flees Home and Co-Habits with Another Man; Husband Detects and Stabs the Paramour

Wang Weifa, a coolie from Ningbo, currently 37 years old, working at a scrap cloth store in Jiangwan's Qimei Road, and his wife, Ding, lived together on Qipu Road. Because Wang's income was limited, their life was extremely difficult, causing Ding to often express dissatisfaction. Ten days ago, Wang Weifa went to work in Jiangwan and only returned home the day before yesterday. Unexpectedly, Ding had disappeared. After a secret investigation, he learned that his wife Ding had eloped with Wang Haifu. Wang Haifu, 33 years old, from Ningbo, worked as a groom at the racecourse on Mahuo Road. After becoming acquainted with Ding, they cohabited at No. 15 Yonghe Lane, Kaifeng Road, living together like husband and wife. Wang Weifa, after learning the truth, was consumed by anger. He went to investigate the night before last and found Ding and Wang Haifu in bed together. He quietly returned. Last night, Wang Weifa hid a knife and went to Wang Haifu's house on Kaifeng Road. When Wang and Ding saw Wang Weifa arrive, they fled to the balcony. Wang Weifa chased after them and stabbed Wang Haifu three times with the knife, causing serious injuries to his arm and left abdomen, with blood gushing out. Someone reported it to the Huishi Police Station, who sent detective Gao Yuqing to arrest the assailant Wang Weifa. The knife was also seized and taken to the police station. The injured man was sent to Baojiang Hospital for treatment. This morning, he was sent to the First Special Court. Attorney Zhang Tianyin of the police station charged him with aggravated assault under Article 278 of the Criminal Law, stating the case and saying that doctors at Baojiang Hospital had confirmed that Wang Haifu's arm was injured, and the left abdomen was even more severely injured, with the omentum protruding. The injuries were dangerous, so he could not be brought to court today. He requested that the case be postponed. Wang Ding also turned herself in, confessing to cohabiting with Wang Haifu since the sixth day of the first lunar month after eloping, because Wang Weifa could not provide for her. She claimed she did not see the stabbing last night. Questioned, Wang Weifa confessed to the stabbing. Judge Tan Xinzhen, after reviewing the testimony, ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody and the case adjourned to the 13th.

Chen Xu, a Woman Accused of Abusing a Maid 142

Chen Xu (age 49), a woman from Qingkou, East Jiaxing Road, Lane 304, No. 23, bought a 10-year-old girl named Yulan from Suzhou as a maid for fifty yuan last April. Wife of Hardware Store Owner Sentenced for Theft 146

Two Months Imprisonment, Three Years Probation

Store Employee Sentenced to Six Months for Transporting Stolen Goods

Wu Tangshi, the wife of Wu Lusheng, owner of Zhenxing Hardware Store at No. 621 Henan Road and No. 491 Mei Bai Ge Road, after having a disagreement with her husband, Wu Lusheng, took 754 yuan in cash and several dozen checks with a face value of 4,916 yuan from the store. She fled with a store employee named Cao Shouzheng, first to Suzhou and then to Wuxi. Wu Lusheng apprehended them at Room 26 of the New World Hotel in Wuxi. He reported it to the Detective Division of the Patrol Bureau, who dispatched detectives Gao Zhenhua and Bao Tan Tian Yuan to Wuxi to bring them back to Shanghai. They were brought before the First Special District Court. Wu Tangshi was released on bail of 5,000 yuan, while Cao was remanded in custody for further questioning. This news was previously reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Fu Lin of the First Special Court continued the hearing in the Second Criminal Court. The Patrol Bureau's lawyer, Qian Xunjiu, stated that after the adjournment, the Patrol Bureau went to the Wuxi Public Security Bureau on April 30 and retrieved the stolen goods. This included 480 yuan in paper money, 120 yuan in fractional currency, 7 silver dollars, 50 single fractional coins, and a diamond ring. The defendant had previously stated that she had a box deposited with her uncle, Sun Fushan, on Gordon Road. The Patrol Bureau investigated Sun's home. Sun claimed ignorance, but his wife stated that Wu Tangshi, her store employee Wang Yugui, and a nanny had indeed deposited a trunk, saying that the store owner was away and that Wu Tangshi had to go to Suzhou, so they were temporarily storing it. The next day, they called Wu Lusheng at the store and told him to come and get it. Wu, along with Wang Yugui and the nanny, then took the trunk away in a cart. Thus, the whereabouts of the trunk were accounted for. Furthermore, it was stated that the checks were given to Wu Wenhua, the owner of the Wu Deyuan Lumber Mill in Xiaodongmen. The Patrol Bureau found that Wu was employed at the Xiangxing Foreign Firm on Beijing Road. Upon investigating the foreign firm, Wu Wenhua stated that Cao Shouzheng had indeed given him 54 checks, asking him to collect them. Eighteen checks, totaling 488 yuan and 52 cents, had already been collected. The remaining 36 checks and the money were handed over to the Patrol Bureau. The plaintiff, Wu Lusheng, originally hired lawyer Yang Linzhi to file a civil suit. However, since the lost items had been recovered and only a small amount was missing, he declared the withdrawal of the civil suit. Subsequently, Sun Fushan, Wang Yugui, and others testified. Cao Shouzheng continued to deny any collusion with the mistress in the theft. After arguments between the Patrol Bureau's lawyer Qian and the defendant's lawyer, the presiding judge announced the verdict: Wu Tangshi was sentenced to two months imprisonment, suspended for three years, for theft; Cao Shouzheng was sentenced to six months imprisonment for transporting stolen goods.

Shanghai National Products Factory Union Discusses Purchasing an Airplane as a Birthday Gift 150

The Shanghai National Products Factory Union convened a meeting yesterday to discuss the issue of purchasing an airplane as a birthday gift, inviting executive and supervisory committee members. Over ten people attended, including Zhang Zilian, Tu Kaizheng, Jiang Zhonghe, Cao Zhigong, Shu Huizhen, Xian Guansheng, Xu Wenbin, Zhou Shixuan, Xu Jianfan, Ma Jisheng, Sun Choucheng, and Ma Xishen. The union has been dedicated to promoting national products. To boost sales of national products, it is essential to strengthen national defense and prevent aggression. Last year, when German Chancellor Hitler celebrated his 44th birthday, the entire nation purchased over 500 airplanes as a birthday gift, greatly benefiting national defense. Provinces, cities, and counties are now initiating similar efforts, and the future results are immeasurable. Therefore, this meeting was convened to discuss fundraising methods. Zhang Zilian stated that if the people do not unite and support their leader, they will be like loose sand, easily bullied. Everyone knows that Chairman Chiang is working hard to govern the country, and we should raise substantial funds to purchase an airplane as a birthday gift to show our support. Zhou Shixuan stated that the Qinkung Shengji Dyeing and Weaving Factory strongly supports this matter and will take the lead in raising funds once the methods are decided. The following resolutions were made:

* Notify all member factories that all staff members should donate at least one day's salary or more. The factory's donation should match the total amount donated by all staff members. Workers who are not members of the union are welcome to donate, limited to one day's wage or more.

* Send letters to various national products organizations, urging them to advocate for this cause.

* Designate the Shanghai Bank as the fundraising agency. Members should send their donations to the bank and notify the union for record-keeping.

Central Savings Society Offers Preferential Treatment to Former Sino-French Savings Society Account Holders 151

Sino-French Savings Society Account Holders Exchanging Passbooks

Not Only No Loss, But Also Preferential Treatment

Since its opening, the Central Savings Society has seen booming business. To facilitate account holders in the interior, the society is establishing branch offices throughout the country. Branches in Tianjin and Beiping are also expected to be established soon. Initially, when the society took over the Sino-French Savings Society, account holders were concerned about potential losses. It has been reported that the society is offering exceptional preferential treatment to former Sino-French Savings Society account holders. Concrete measures have been formulated and communicated to all account holders. Those who hold prize-winning savings passbooks from the Sino-French Savings Society can exchange them for new passbooks from the society without incurring any losses. As for special fixed deposit savings, the society is allowing account holders to retain their original prize-winning savings amounts and exchange them for new passbooks. Regarding ordinary savings accounts from the Sino-French Savings Society, those that have matured can be withdrawn in cash or continued to be deposited with the Central Trust Bureau. Those that have not matured will be deposited with the Central Trust Bureau, earning interest according to the savings regulations. It is said that exchanging for new passbooks is most advantageous for former Sino-French Savings Society account holders. Previously, a monthly payment of 15 yuan in Sino-French accounts only offered a top prize of 10,000 yuan. Under the new society's regulations, a monthly payment of 12 yuan offers the hope of a top prize of 25,000 yuan. Moreover, since the society is newly established, the number of participating numbers in the lottery is currently less than 50,000, thus increasing the chances of winning. Furthermore, account holders can still win prizes in the fifteenth year, even without making payments. Under the Sino-French Savings Society's system, participation in the lottery ceased in the final year. There are also various other preferential measures, such as reduced payments for account holders who prepay their savings for six months or a year. Additionally, the refund amount upon withdrawal is higher than that of the Sino-French Savings Society. The society's bonus fund accumulates compound interest annually. Even if account holders withdraw midway, the unissued bonuses will also accrue interest. Therefore, the bonus earned by account holders who complete the term is several times higher than that of the Sino-French Savings Society. The society has a fund of 5 million yuan and is a state-run institution with the sole purpose of encouraging national savings. The regulations are designed to benefit account holders. Therefore, former Sino-French Savings Society account holders are eagerly exchanging their old passbooks for new ones.

Central Bank Inspection Report 152

Central Bank Currency Exchange Note Issuance Reserve 280th Inspection Report: In accordance with Article 13 of the Central Bank Law, this council is responsible for inspecting the Central Bank's currency exchange note issuance and reserve funds. Today, May 2, 1936, the 280th inspection was held at the bank's Issuance Bureau. The inspection results are reported as follows: (A) Total face value of currency exchange notes issued: 26,794,2781 silver dollars, including 24,204,3505 silver dollar notes and 2,589,9276 auxiliary currency notes. Total value of currency exchange note reserve funds: 26,794,2781 silver dollars, including 18,355,9681 silver dollars in cash. This cash reserve is held at the bank's Issuance Bureau, branch offices, and sub-branches, totaling 15,139,4153.71 silver dollars, and held in other banks, totaling 3,216,5527.29 silver dollars. The collateral reserve is equivalent to 8,438,3100 silver dollars. (B) Total face value of customs gold currency exchange notes issued: 373,324.70 yuan. Total value of customs gold currency exchange note reserve funds: 373,324.70 yuan. This reserve fund includes 7,351.95 taels of bullion, which, at a fixed price of 5.0779, equals 373,324.70 yuan in customs gold. According to Article 22 of the Central Bank Law, the cash reserve must be at least 60%, with the remainder being held in legal collateral. The inspection results show that the cash reserve exceeds 60%, and the collateral reserve is within 40%, in compliance with the regulations. This report is hereby submitted. May 4, 1936. Chairman of the Central Bank Supervisory Council, Li Fuxun, Supervisors Xie Mengjun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jilong.

Pushan Villa's Charity Report for April 153

Shanghai Pushan Villa's charity report for April 1936, covering both the Chinese and foreign concession areas. A total of 190 large coffins and 3,270 small coffins were collected for burial. 1,670 coffins of various sizes were provided. This included 37 large coffins and 2,003 small coffins collected by the main villa, along with the exhumation of 7 sets of bones. The Xiejiao Nanshi branch villa and various charitable halls in the French Concession collected 622 small coffins. The Public Concession's police stations and the Health Bureau consulted on unclaimed children's corpses and bodies from various hospitals within the concession, resulting in the collection of 134 large coffins and 623 small coffins. The Lianyi Charity Association collected 5 large coffins and 15 small coffins. The Women and Children's Relief Association Orphanage collected 3 large coffins. The Red Cross Society First Hospital collected 4 large coffins. Tongren Hospital collected 3 large coffins. The Epidemic Hospital collected 2 large coffins and 1 small coffin. Tongde Hospital collected 3 small coffins. The Pushan Obstetrics Hospital of the White Cross Society on Xinmin Road in Zhabei provided medical consultations and medication to a total of 3,077 patients. It has been observed that the recent erratic weather and the prevalence of smallpox have led to a higher number of deaths, making the villa's burial work, medical consultations, and medication distribution even busier. However, the expenses are enormous and the funds are strained. We earnestly hope that philanthropists from all walks of life will provide assistance to help alleviate the situation.

The Ancient Meaning of New Life 161

By Zhang Shouyong

Everyone thinks that the three characters "New Life" are a new term or a colloquialism. Calling it a colloquialism, it is indeed a colloquialism. Village women work all day long and say to each other, "Is today's life finished?" What is called "life" is their work. Because they cannot live without this work, they call work "life." When asked by a scholar what the two characters "life" come from, some are speechless and cannot answer. I tell them, "Have you read Mencius? 'The people cannot live without water and fire,' which speaks of the importance of life." What the village women say is based on Mencius. Today, everyone knows about life, but they do not read Mencius thoroughly. How can they neglect what is said to be "gained, then there is life; lost, then there is death"? How can they talk about the New Life? Nothing is more important to life than water and fire. Everyone knows how to seek water and fire, but they do not know how to seek propriety, justice, integrity, and shame. Is this not valuing water and fire over propriety, justice, integrity, and shame? Qi, a state; one country; Guan Zhong, the assistant to the hegemon, still knew to teach the people that if the four cardinal virtues are not upheld, the country will perish. The four cardinal virtues are propriety, justice, integrity, and shame. Today, in such a large China, the descendants of the enlightened Yellow Emperor, with the knowledge and skills passed down by generations of sages, leave teachings to our descendants, and yet they are not as enlightened as countries that were civilized thousands of years later and are located overseas, who still know how to恪守礼法. What shame could be greater! Moreover, the system passed down in our country begins with ritual education. In the past, the laws were based on ritual education. To guide them with ritual is to include propriety, justice, integrity, and shame. Ritual is reason, that is, order. Today's so-called守秩序is ritual. Where does the phrase 守秩序come from? When asked by a scholar, they are speechless and do not know. I tell them again, "Have you read the Book of Documents? It says, 'Heaven orders with ritual,' which is what is called秩. Have you read Mencius? There is order between elders and juniors, which is what is called序. To run ahead of elders is called不弟." To run ahead of elders is a small matter of disrespect, but it is called不弟. Therefore,守秩序has always been the beginning of ritual education for ancient people. Someone may ask, "Does the so-called cleaning movement today exist in ancient times?" I say, "Mencius said, 'Enter their borders, open up the fields and manage them well, then there will be celebration.' This is the greatest kind of cleaning. Zizhang said, 'Sprinkling and sweeping, responding and retreating, then it is acceptable.' This is the smallest kind of cleaning." Wang Yangming extended it by saying, "Sprinkling and sweeping, responding and retreating, the essence enters the spirit, small sprinkling and sweeping, responding and retreating. It is said that the essence enters the spirit." It can be seen that everything starts from the small things, and the presence or absence of spirit can be seen in them. Someone may also ask, "Is there anything to say about keeping time?" I say, "Confucius said, 'A man without trustworthiness, I do not know what he is good for. A large cart without a yoke, a small cart without a linchpin, how can I travel?'" Today, when we look at meetings, they are often delayed, not knowing how much time is wasted. Keeping time is valuing time, and it is keeping Confucius's戒that a man without trustworthiness is unknowable! Someone may also say, "What are the bases for today's so-called three transformations?" I say: Confucius emphasized military affairs at the Jiaogu meeting, and the arrangements were unhurried. If preparations are not made in advance, how could one not humiliate the country! His saying that military affairs are something he has not learned was only addressed to Duke Ling of Wei. Wei did not need to use troops, so he replied that he had not learned it. This is the meaning of "I will not participate in fighting tigers on foot or crossing rivers without a boat." What he usually paid attention to was war. Zengzi said, "One can entrust the life of a hundred miles, and one cannot be taken away at a time of great moral crisis." Is this not military transformation? What Zilu called "being able to make them brave and knowing the principles" included a wide range of things, and military discipline was one aspect of it. One can be used only after knowing the principles, and one cannot be used if one does not know the principles. If everyone maintains military transformation, then everyone will know the principles. Furthermore, to take the Book of Great Learning, from illuminating virtue, to loving the people, and stopping at perfection, its final chapter says, "There is a way to create wealth; those who produce it are many, those who consume it are few; those who work on it are quick, those who use it are leisurely." Those who produce and make it should take "many" and "quick," while those who consume and use it should take "few" and "leisurely." The economic principles of ancient and modern times, both domestic and foreign, are no different from this. Is this not production transformation! Scholars avoid talking about financial management and consider not managing production to be noble. Therefore, they are poor and sick. Production transformation is the foundation of governance. 行有餘力、則以學文, Zhu Xi said that文 is the literature of the Book of Songs and the Six Arts.游於藝, 吾不試, Therefore, Art is especially valued by the ancients. What the Song Confucianists called being vibrant, if it is not artistic化, then the spirit cannot be flexible, and it is not just fine arts! Mr. Chiang has a thorough understanding of the situation in ancient and modern times, and he has combined it with the New Life Movement of Confucius. Since the beginning, the old bad habits have been transformed by the new human heart, and they have been deeply affected. As the poem says, "Zhou is an old country, but its destiny is new." New is to reform the old. Confucius said, "Reviewing the old and knowing the new," Zhu Xi said, "The old is what was heard in the past, and the new is what is gained today. It must be based on what was heard in the past to have new gains." I hope that people all over the country will seek newness based on ancient meanings, so that the national spirit can return to the old times of Tang, Yu, and the Three Dynasties, and all actions will be mindful of the principle of物競天擇,优胜劣收, to reform and innovate to seek today's survival. Then the China of the Book of Songs, the Book of Documents, the Book of Rites, and the Book of Music, uniting scholars, farmers, artisans, and merchants to rise up together, will surpass the civilized countries of Europe and America. The inscription on Tang's basin says, "If you can make it new one day, make it new every day, and again make it new." Overcoming national difficulties is here, and establishing the foundation of the country is also here! Fellow countrymen, gentlemen, let us encourage each other!

Record of the Second Test for the World Games Track and Field Training Class 164

Wu Bixian Sets New High Jump Record

Reaching a Height of 1.871 Meters. Fu Baolu, Dong Shuquan, and Wang Shilin Barely Qualify

(Special Dispatch from Beiping) The second performance test for the track and field athletes training for the World Games in our country was held at the Qinghua University Educational Field in Beiping at 4 PM on the 4th. The weather was unfavorable that day, with wind and sand affecting performance to a considerable extent. In addition to the 22 athletes who had already reported, Li Peigen, a renowned 800-meter runner, also participated in the test. Before 3 PM, the sports field was already packed with spectators. The test began promptly at 4 PM. Except for Jin Changxian, Sun Yueming, and Zhang Kan, who voluntarily gave up their rights, Lin Shaozhou, Liu Changchun, Wang He, Yang Henghuan, and Liu Shikui, who requested leave due to illness, and Dong Hanwen, who was absent due to other matters, only 14 people participated in the test. The events included 100 meters, 200 meters, 400 meters, high jump, triple jump, pole vault, shot put, discus, and javelin. The 800 meters, 1500 meters, 10,000 meters, long jump, high hurdles, and middle hurdles were not held due to a lack of participants. As a result, Wu Bixian set a new national record in the high jump with a height of 1.871 meters. Dong Shuzhao in the 400 meters, Fu Baolu in the pole vault, and Wang Shilin in the triple jump all achieved qualifying scores. In total, 11 people qualified in the two tests. The next test is scheduled for 4 PM on the 11th of this month, still at Qinghua University. Ma Yuehan has already sent a letter to Shen Siliang urging the payment of the national sports association subsidy for the 11 qualified athletes, which should be remitted to Beiping within days. The results of the second test for the track and field pre-selection training class are recorded below:

Breaking the National Record

The high jump participants were still Wu Bixian and Liu Mengji. Starting at 1.76 meters, Wu cleared 1.82 meters on his first attempt, while Liu struggled and jumped four times to clear it. When the height was raised to 1.871 meters, Liu withdrew, and Wu Bixian cleared it on his first attempt, although his left hand touched the bar, fortunately without knocking it down. This jump broke his own national record of 1.82 meters. When the height was raised to 1.93 meters, he failed to clear it due to fatigue, but he came very close.

Achieving Standard Scores: In the 400 meters, Jia Lianren and Dong Shuzhao competed against each other. They finished at the same time, with no clear winner, in 52.4 seconds, exceeding the standard record of 53 seconds.

Only Fu Baolu participated in the pole vault. Wang He did not participate due to illness. Fu cleared 3.63 meters and then rested.

Yang Henghuan did not participate in the triple jump due to illness. The audience thought that the event would be canceled, so they were about to leave when Wang Shilin, known for his triple jump skills, came to participate in the test. After several jumps, he cleared the standard record of 14 meters with a jump of 14.01 meters. Since there was no one to compete with him, he did not make a final effort.

Mediocre Performances: Only Zhang Lingjia and Cheng Mengping participated in the discus throw. Zhang Lingjia took first place with a throw of 36.05 meters, and Cheng Mengping took second place with a throw of 34.90 meters. Liu Changchun did not participate in the 200 meters due to a leg injury. Only Dai Shuguo and Zhang Yinming participated, accompanied by the newly arrived Li Peigen. Dai Shuguo finished first in 24 seconds, and Zhang Yinming followed in 25 seconds. Chen Baoqiu, after setting a new record of 12.745 meters in the shot put and discus in the first test, was excited and delighted every day. He happily participated again today, with Cheng Mengping competing alongside him. Chen's performance of 12.86 meters did not improve and was actually a step back compared to his first test. Cheng Mengping's score was 11.57 meters. In the javelin throw, Peng Yongxin, Zhou Changxing, and Cheng Mengping competed again. Peng Yongxin took first place with a throw of 49.08 meters, Zhou Changxing took second place with 48.30 meters, and Cheng Mengping took third place with 47.30 meters. Only Zhang Yinming and Dai Shuguo participated in the 100 meters, accompanied by Lin Shaozhou and Cheng Mengping. The score was 11.8 seconds, a decline compared to the result of 11.4 seconds in the last test.

Jiangda Volleyball Tournament Ends Yesterday, Fudan Wins Championship Again 165

Winning All Three Matches in Straight Sets

Chizhi Defeats Guanghua Yesterday to Claim Second Place

The 9th Jiangda Volleyball Tournament concluded yesterday with two matches: Fudan vs. Jinan and Chizhi vs. Guanghua, held at the Jinan and Guanghua courts respectively. Fudan defeated Jinan in straight sets, winning all three matches and retaining the championship. Chizhi also defeated Guanghua 3-0 to claim second place. The match details and overall results of the tournament are as follows:

Fudan vs. Jinan: The match between Fudan and Jinan took place at the Jinan court at 3 PM yesterday. Jinan took the initiative after the start, scoring the first point. Fudan responded quickly, and with Yuan Zejian's agile performance, Jinan took a 5-2 lead. Fudan's Chen Zongqiang unleashed powerful shots, quickly scoring ten points. The score went back and forth until 20-13, when Fudan's Zhou Dayun scored again, easily winning the first set 21-13. In the second set, Jinan once again took the offensive, scoring the first point. Zhou Dayun calmly scored four consecutive points. After a 12-12 tie, Jinan's defense gradually loosened, and Fudan seized the opportunity to win again 21-15. In the third set, Fudan did not easily let up. Zhou Dayun delivered a spectacular performance, scoring many points on his own, always finding unexpected and effective ways to defeat the enemy. Jinan also changed its tactics and had a turning point, leading 7-6 and 11-10 at one point. However, their overall coordination was not as tight and skillful as Fudan's, and they ultimately failed, resulting in a score of 21-16. Overall, Fudan defeated Jinan in straight sets, winning the Jiangda Volleyball Championship this year.

Jinan Team:

Kuang Yaoya, Kuang Yaoji, Deng Xilin,

Yuan Zejian, Zhang Minzhi, Situ Shan,

Liu Boxi, Situ Ze, Chen Nianjin

Fudan Team:

Tan Lijian, Chen Zongqi, Guan Xun'an,

Zhou Dayun, Li Yaohua, Zeng Qixiang,

Zhou Jieming, Qiu Guangxue, Chen Bocai

Chizhi vs. Guanghua: The match between Chizhi and Guanghua was refereed by Chen Deqian and started at 3 PM. Guanghua served first and scored one point. Chizhi was not willing to be outdone. Huang Yufu unleashed a high pressure attack, scoring two points. Wang Shen scored two own goals, and Yu Hewen rose in the middle, scoring two consecutive points. The score then tied several times. However, Chizhi's defense was tight, and they relied on Huang Yufu's smashing attacks, which often left Guanghua helpless. When the score reached 18-12, Guanghua's momentum was strong, and they tied the score, showing signs of a comeback. However, due to repeated own goals, they ultimately failed. The result was 21-18, with Chizhi winning. In the second set, Guanghua once again scored first. Chizhi's Mai Zhihong made a powerful attack, and Huang Yufu assisted from the side, quickly increasing the score. Guanghua's Situ Mu also made near-net pressure hits, succeeding in scoring points. The score tied at 10-10. Chizhi's Huang Yufu was a general, using feints and achieving his goals. At 20-18, Guanghua fought bravely, putting on an amazing performance, but because they had lost too many points, they lost again 21-18. Guanghua, having lost two consecutive sets, was not discouraged and still concentrated on fighting. After the start of the third set, they scored one point first, but Chizhi took the opportunity to score seven consecutive points. After that, Guanghua never recovered. Chizhi's Huang Yufu made high pressure attacks and near-net pressure hits, all succeeding. They won again 21-18, with a total score of 2-0, Chizhi winning by a large margin.

All-Around Competition Discontinued

The 9th Jiangda Track and Field Meet will be held on the 23rd and 24th of this month at Guanghua University. The announcement is recorded as follows:

Championships: Divided into men's field events, men's track events, and women's track and field events (championships will be canceled and treated as exhibition matches if fewer than three schools participate). (Men's Field Events) Shot Put, Discus Throw, Javelin Throw, Long Jump, High Jump, Pole Vault, Triple Jump. (Men's Track Events) 100 meters, 200 meters, 400 meters, 800 meters, 1500 meters, 10,000 meters, High Hurdles (110 meters), Middle Hurdles (400 meters). (Women's Track and Field) 50 meters, 100 meters, 200 meters, Long Jump, High Jump, Shot Put (8 pounds), Softball Throw, Far (12 o'clock), 200-meter Relay Race.

The all-around competition will be discontinued this year.

Each member can enter a maximum of four athletes in each event.

Each athlete can participate in a maximum of three events in track or field events. The combined number of track and field events an athlete participates in cannot exceed four.

The top four athletes in each event's final will be awarded points, with the first-place finisher receiving 5 points, the second-place finisher receiving 3 points, the third-place finisher receiving 2 points, and the fourth-place finisher receiving 1 point. If members have the same score, the member with more first-place finishes will win the championship, and so on.

The registration deadline is the 18th of this month.

Unless otherwise specified by the association, the rules of the National Games will be adopted for the competition.

Education News

National Postal and Telecommunications Bureau to Establish Staff Remedial Education Classes 171

(Nanjing, 6th) To improve the knowledge of postal and telecommunications staff, the Ministry of Communications has ordered all postal and telecommunications bureaus nationwide to establish staff remedial education classes after the summer vacation. It is stipulated that all staff, except senior technicians, postal workers, and first-class telegraph operators, must enroll in the classes. They will be divided into senior and junior levels, according to their academic abilities. Teachers will be senior staff members within the bureau, and they will not be paid extra. The course will last for two years. Those with outstanding performance will be rewarded by the Ministry.

School Survey

Overview of the German School in Shanghai (3) 178

— Hu Zuyin

3. Administrative Overview

Administrative Organization: Under the current German national conditions, the administration of the school naturally adopts a centralized system. The School Affairs Committee is responsible for matters such as the custody of school property and the receipt and expenditure of funds. The School Affairs Committee is elected by the German Community Corporation. The committee consists of six people. First, the Community Corporation elects one person as the chairman of the committee, and then the chairman hires four German residents as committee members, plus the principal of the school as an ex-officio member, totaling six people. According to the principal of the school, this method imitates Hitler's system of total control.

The principal of the school is selected by the German Ministry of Education, which proposes three or four people with educational knowledge and experience, and asks the School Affairs Committee to select one person from these candidates. Teachers are also hired using the same method; of course, the principal can participate in the School Affairs Committee's opinions on hiring teachers. Many affairs of the school, such as the repair of school buildings and the receipt and expenditure of regular expenses, are managed by the School Affairs Committee; therefore, the principal can concentrate all efforts on presiding over the educational matters within the school. Also, because the number of students is small, the principal can independently preside over all school affairs without the need to establish other staff to assist.

Financial Income: The school's budget for this year is 85,000 yuan. The income includes: tuition fees of approximately 50,000 yuan; subsidies from the Community Corporation of 24,000 yuan; subsidies from the Public Concession工部局 of 7,000 yuan; and donations from other German residents of approximately 4,000 yuan. The expenditure includes: salaries for teachers and staff and wages for school workers of approximately 70,000 yuan, accounting for 82% of the total expenditure; other regular expenses of approximately 15,000 yuan, accounting for 18% of the total expenditure. The tuition fees paid by students at all levels vary: kindergarten students pay 130 yuan per year; primary school students pay 165 yuan per year; middle school students pay 220 yuan per year for the first six years and 600 yuan per year for the last three years. According to the principal of the school, there are not many German children who graduate from the school's middle school. Most students leave the school after completing six years of middle school. This situation is because the tuition fees for the last three years of middle school are too expensive, and many students drop out of school halfway to work; there are also many students who return to their home country to continue their studies.

4. Emphasis on Free Discussion

One of the characteristics of the school's teaching is its emphasis on free discussion among students. The school's teaching purpose is to develop students' judgment and character. Free discussion is a good way to develop judgment. Free discussion can expand children's knowledge and enable children to acquire and understand various new ideas. Therefore, the school's teachers encourage children to engage in free discussion in primary school; when children are learning reading, writing, arithmetic, and other subjects, they can freely discuss the knowledge and skills in the subjects, and the teachers provide necessary guidance. The result of free discussion can enable children to experience many new insights and express many creative works in posture, language, drawing, or spelling.

In middle school, the spirit of free discussion is even more emphasized. The curriculum of the middle school department is relatively deep and broad, so middle school students need a more detailed understanding of the deep and broad curriculum. Free discussion is an important way to develop middle school students' comprehension. Middle school students can stimulate each other's thinking or exchange research insights in free discussion. The school further implements self-study guidance methods for students in the top two classes of the middle school department, allowing students to study automatically, and teachers are often in a guiding position.

Jiangsu Social Education Management Personnel Conference 182

Decides on Various Guidance and Promotion Methods

(Zhenjiang Correspondence) The Jiangsu Education Department convened a conference of social education management personnel from the province on the 6th. Attendees included Zhao Hongqian, director of the Zhenjiang and other eight provincial people's education centers, and Wu Jianzhen presided over the meeting. The following are the matters resolved that can be announced: On the issue of how provincial social education institutions should allocate guidance to social education institutions in various counties, it was resolved that: 1. County stadiums should be guided by provincial stadiums; 2. County libraries should be guided by provincial libraries; 3. People's schools, experimental agricultural education centers, combined political education experimental zones, and parks in various counties should be guided by provincial people's education centers. Regarding how the provincial people's education center should conduct civic training, it was resolved that: The provincial people's education center should select one autonomous region in the county where it is located and cooperate with the local county government to establish a central people's school. The methods and plans should be drafted in conjunction with the local county government and submitted to the department for approval and implementation. Regarding how livelihood education should be promoted, it was resolved that: The provincial people's education center should actively carry out the following tasks as needed: 1. Assist in the breeding and promotion of improved varieties of major crops and major livestock products in the guidance area; 2. Promote and guide cooperative businesses and other economic organizations; 3. Promote rural sideline industries and agricultural product processing in the area; 4. Promote vocational training (such as holding agricultural seminars). Regarding how film education should be promoted, it was resolved that: Director Zhao Hongqian should be asked to draft implementation measures and submit them to the guidance agency for review and then to the department for adoption and implementation. Regarding how rural youth should be cultivated, it was resolved that: Zhao Guangtao, President Gao Jian, and Mr. Yu Qingtang should be asked to draft detailed measures and submit them to the guidance agency for review and then to the department for adoption and implementation. Regarding how guidance work should be regulated, it was resolved that: Director Niu Changyao, Director Zhao Hongqian, and Director Wang Mengfan should be asked to appropriately modify the original measures and submit them to the guidance agency for review and then to the department for adoption and implementation. Regarding how literacy education should be promoted, it was resolved that: The provincial people's education center should provide guidance to various counties on compulsory literacy at any time and actively carry out literacy education in the experimental area. The meeting adjourned at 4:00 p.m.
